s[1])) {\n    return { width: parts[0], height: parts[1] };\n  }\n  return { width: 720, height: 1280 };\n}\n\n/** Upload remote video URL to Supabase Storage */\nasync function streamVideoToStorage(videoUrl: string): Promise<string | null> {\n  try {\n    const response = await fetch(videoUrl);\n    if (!response.ok) {\n      console.error(`Fetch video failed: ${response.status}`);\n      return null;\n    }\n    const contentType = response.headers.get("content-type") ?? "video/mp4";\n    const ext = contentType.includes("mp4") ? "mp4" : "mp4";\n    const filePath = `uploads/${crypto.randomUUID()}.${ext}`;\n    const { data, error } = await supabase.storage\n      .from("generated-videos")\n      .upload(filePath, response.body!, {\n        contentType,\n        cacheControl: "no-cache",\n        upsert: false,\n      });\n    if (error) {\n      console.error("Upload to storage error:", error);\n      return null;\n    }\n    const { data: urlData } = supabase.storage.from("generated-videos").getPublicUrl(filePath);\n    return urlData.publicUrl;\n  } catch (err) {\n    console.error("streamVideoToStorage error:", err);\n    return null;\n  }\n}\n\nserve(async (req) => {\n  if (req.method === "OPTIONS") {\n    return new Response(null, { status: 204, headers: corsHeaders() });\n  }\n\n  if (req.method !== "POST") {\n    return new Response(\n      JSON.stringify({ error: "Method Not Allowed" }),\n      { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },\n    );\n  }\n\n  let body: Record<string, unknown>;\n  try {\n    body = await req.json();\n  } catch {\n    return new Response(\n      JSON.stringify({ error: "Invalid request body" }),\n      { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },\n    );\n  }\n\n  // Get Jimeng API key from request body (user-provided) or env fallback\n  const userApiKey = (body.jimeng_api_key as string) ?? "";\n  const envApiKey = Deno.env.get("JIMENG_API_KEY") ?? "";\n  const apiKey = userApiKey || envApiKey;\n\n  if (!apiKey) {\n    return new Response(\n      JSON.stringify({ error: "未配置即梦 API Key，请在设置中填写" }),\n      { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },\n    );\n  }\n\n  const prompt = (body.prompt as string) ?? "";\n  if (!prompt) {\n    return new Response(\n      JSON.stringify({ error: "缺少 prompt 参数" }),\n      { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },\n    );\n  }\n\n  const size = (body.size as string) ?? "720x1280";\n  const seconds = (body.seconds as number) ?? 8;\n  const inputReferenceUrl = (body.input_reference_url as string) ?? undefined;\n  const mode = (body.mode as string) ?? "text-to-video";\n  // Jimeng model name; user can override via request body\n  const modelName = (body.model as string) ?? "jimeng-video-generate-3.0";\n\n  const { width, height } = parseSize(size);\n\n  // Build upstream request for Jimeng / Ark platform\n  // Volcengine Ark imaginations API (OpenAI-compatible)\n  const upstreamBody: Record<string, unknown> = {\n    model: modelName,\n    prompt,\n    width,\n    height,\n    duration: seconds,\n  };\n  if (inputReferenceUrl) {\n    upstreamBody.image_url = inputReferenceUrl;\n  }\n  // Optional: FPS, seed, etc.\n  const fps = (body.fps as number) ?? undefined;\n  if (fps !== undefined) upstreamBody.fps = fps;\n\n  // Primary endpoint: Ark imaginations API (OpenAI-compatible)\n  // Try with user-provided model, then fallback models\n  const models = [modelName, "jimeng-video-generate-3.0", "jimeng-video-3.0", "video-generation"];\n  const endpoints = [\n    "https://ark.cn-beijing.volces.com/api/v3/imaginations/generations",\n    "https://ark.cn-beijing.volces.com/api/v3/videos/generations",\n  ];\n\n  let lastError = "";\n  for (const endpoint of endpoints) {\n    for (const m of models) {\n      try {\n        const reqBody = { ...upstreamBody, model: m };\n        const upstream = await fetch(endpoint, {\n          method: "POST",\n          headers: {\n            "Content-Type": "application/json",\n            "Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,\n          },\n          body: JSON.stringify(reqBody),\n        });\n\n        const result = await upstream.json();\n\n        if (!upstream.ok) {\n          const msg = result.error?.message ?? result.message ?? JSON.stringify(result);\n          lastError = `${endpoint} model=${m} 错误 (${upstream.status}): ${msg}`;\n          console.error(lastError);\n          // If it\'s a model-not-found error, try next model; otherwise try next endpoint\n          const msgLower = String(msg).toLowerCase();\n          if (msgLower.includes("model") || msgLower.includes("not found") || msgLower.includes("不存在")) {\n            continue; // try next model\n          }\n          break; // try next endpoint\n        }\n\n        // Success path\n        const jobId = result.id ?? result.data?.id ?? result.job_id ?? result.task_id;\n        if (jobId) {\n          return new Response(\n            JSON.stringify({ videoId: String(jobId), status: result.status ?? "processing" }),\n            { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },\n          );\n        }\n\n        // If response contains a direct video URL\n        const directVideoUrl = result.video_url ?? result.data?.video_url ?? result.url;\n        if (directVideoUrl) {\n          const publicUrl = await streamVideoToStorage(String(directVideoUrl));\n          return new Response(\n            JSON.stringify({\n              videoId: `direct_${crypto.randomUUID()}`,\n              status: "completed",\n              video_url: publicUrl ?? directVideoUrl,\n              publicUrl: publicUrl ?? directVideoUrl,\n            }),\n            { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },\n          );\n        }\n\n        lastError = `未知响应格式: ${JSON.stringify(result).slice(0, 200)}`;\n      } catch (err) {\n        lastError = `请求 ${endpoint} model=${m} 失败: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}`;\n        console.error(lastError);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // All endpoints failed\n  return new Response(\n    JSON.stringify({ error: `即梦视频生成失败: ${lastError}` }),\n    { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },\n  );\n});\n'}]}

import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts";
import { createClient } from "https://esm.sh/@supabase/supabase-js@2";

const supabase = createClient(
  Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_URL")!,
  Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY")!,
);

function corsHeaders(): Record<string, string> {
  return {
    "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "POST, OPTIONS",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type, Authorization",
  };
}

/** Upload remote image URL to Supabase Storage */
async function streamImageToStorage(imageUrl: string): Promise<string | null> {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(imageUrl);
    if (!response.ok) {
      console.error(`Fetch image failed: ${response.status}`);
      return null;
    }
    const contentType = response.headers.get("content-type") ?? "image/png";
    const ext = contentType.includes("jpg") || contentType.includes("jpeg") ? "jpg" : "png";
    const filePath = `uploads/${crypto.randomUUID()}.${ext}`;
    const { error } = await supabase.storage
      .from("generated-videos")
      .upload(filePath, response.body!, {
        contentType,
        cacheControl: "no-cache",
        upsert: false,
      });
    if (error) {
      console.error("Upload to storage error:", error);
      return null;
    }
    const { data: urlData } = supabase.storage.from("generated-videos").getPublicUrl(filePath);
    return urlData.publicUrl;
  } catch (err) {
    console.error("streamImageToStorage error:", err);
    return null;
  }
}

serve(async (req) => {
  if (req.method === "OPTIONS") {
    return new Response(null, { status: 204, headers: corsHeaders() });
  }

import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts";
import { createClient } from "https://esm.sh/@supabase/supabase-js@2";

const supabase = createClient(
  Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_URL")!,
  Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY")!,
);

function corsHeaders(): Record<string, string> {
  return {
    "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "POST, OPTIONS",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type, Authorization",
  };
}

/** HMAC-SHA256 */
async function hmacSha256(key: ArrayBuffer, data: string): Promise<ArrayBuffer> {
  const cryptoKey = await crypto.subtle.importKey(
    "raw",
    key,
    { name: "HMAC", hash: "SHA-256" },
    false,
    ["sign"],
  );
  return crypto.subtle.sign("HMAC", cryptoKey, new TextEncoder().encode(data));
}

/** Hex encode */
function hexEncode(buf: ArrayBuffer): string {
  return Array.from(new Uint8Array(buf))
    .map((b) => b.toString(16).padStart(2, "0"))
    .join("");
}

/** Hash with SHA-256 */
async function sha256Hash(data: string): Promise<string> {
  const buf = await crypto.subtle.digest("SHA-256", new TextEncoder().encode(data));
  return hexEncode(buf);
}

/**
 * Build Volcengine Authorization header using HMAC-SHA256 signing.
 */
async function buildAuthorization(
  ak: string,
  sk: string,
  method: string,
  uri: string,
  query: string,
  headers: Record<string, string>,
  payload: string,
): Promise<string> {
  const date = (headers["X-Date"] ?? headers["x-date"] ?? "").trim();
  if (!date) throw new Error("Missing X-Date header for signing");
  const dateShort = date.slice(0, 8);
  const region = "cn-north-1";
  const service = "cv";

  const signedHeaders = Object.keys(headers).map((k) => k.toLowerCase()).sort().join(";");

  const canonicalHeaders = Object.entries(headers)
    .sort(([a], [b]) => a.localeCompare(b))
    .map(([k, v]) => `${k.toLowerCase()}:${v.trim()}\n`)
    .join("");

  const payloadHash = await sha256Hash(payload);

  const canonicalRequest = [
    method,
    uri,
    query,
    canonicalHeaders,
    signedHeaders,
    payloadHash,
  ].join("\n");

  const algorithm = "HMAC-SHA256";
  const credentialScope = `${dateShort}/${region}/${service}/request`;
  const canonicalRequestHash = await sha256Hash(canonicalRequest);

  const stringToSign = `${algorithm}\n${date}\n${credentialScope}\n${canonicalRequestHash}`;

  let kDate = await hmacSha256(new TextEncoder().encode(sk), dateShort);
  let kRegion = await hmacSha256(kDate, region);
  let kService = await hmacSha256(kRegion, service);
  let kSigning = await hmacSha256(kService, "request");
  const signature = hexEncode(await hmacSha256(kSigning, stringToSign));

  return `${algorithm} Credential=${ak}/${credentialScope}, SignedHeaders=${signedHeaders}, Signature=${signature}`;
}

/** Upload remote image to Supabase Storage */
async function uploadImageToStorage(imageUrl: string): Promise<string | null> {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(imageUrl);
    if (!response.ok) {
      console.error(`Fetch image failed: ${response.status}`);
      return null;
    }
    const contentType = response.headers.get("content-type") ?? "image/png";
    const ext = contentType.includes("jpg") || contentType.includes("jpeg") ? "jpg" : "png";
    const filePath = `uploads/${crypto.randomUUID()}.${ext}`;
    const { data, error } = await supabase.storage
      .from("generated-videos")
      .upload(filePath, response.body!, {
        contentType,
        cacheControl: "no-cache",
        upsert: false,
      });
    if (error) {
      console.error("Upload to storage error:", error);
      return null;
    }
    const { data: urlData } = supabase.storage.from("generated-videos").getPublicUrl(filePath);
    return urlData.publicUrl;
  } catch (err) {
    console.error("uploadImageToStorage error:", err);
    return null;
  }
}

serve(async (req: Request): Promise<Response> => {
  if (req.method === "OPTIONS") {
    return new Response(null, { status: 204, headers: corsHeaders() });
  }

  if (req.method !== "POST") {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: "Method Not Allowed" }),
      { status: 405, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
    );
  }

  let accessKeyId = "";
  let secretAccessKey = "";
  let prompt = "";
  let size = "1024x1024";

  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    accessKeyId = (body.access_key_id as string) ?? "";
    secretAccessKey = (body.secret_access_key as string) ?? "";
    prompt = (body.prompt as string) ?? "";
    size = (body.size as string) ?? "1024x1024";
  } catch {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: "Invalid request body" }),
      { status: 400, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
    );
  }

  if (!accessKeyId || !secretAccessKey) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: "缺少 Access Key ID 或 Secret Access Key" }),
      { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
    );
  }

  if (!prompt) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: "缺少 prompt 参数" }),
      { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
    );
  }

  const parts = size.split("x").map((s) => parseInt(s.trim(), 10));
  const width = parts.length === 2 && !isNaN(parts[0]) ? parts[0] : 1024;
  const height = parts.length === 2 && !isNaN(parts[1]) ? parts[1] : 1024;
  const area = width * height;

  const endpoint = "https://visual.volcengineapi.com";
  const uri = "/";
  const query = "Action=CVSync2AsyncSubmitTask&Version=2022-08-31";
  const payload = JSON.stringify({
    req_key: "jimeng_t2i_v40",
    prompt,
    size: area,
    width,
    height,
    force_single: true,
  });

  const now = new Date();
  const xDate = now.toISOString().replace(/[:\-]|\.\d{3}/g, "").slice(0, 15) + "Z";
  const headers: Record<string, string> = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Host": "visual.volcengineapi.com",
    "X-Date": xDate,
  };

  try {
    const authorization = await buildAuthorization(
      accessKeyId,
      secretAccessKey,
      "POST",
      uri,
      query,
      headers,
      payload,
    );

    const resp = await fetch(`${endpoint}${uri}?${query}`, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        ...headers,
        "Authorization": authorization,
      },
      body: payload,
      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(30000),
    });

    const result = await resp.json();

    // 火山引擎错误码处理
    if (result.code !== 10000 && result.code !== "10000") {
      const code = result?.ResponseMetadata?.Error?.Code ?? result?.code ?? "";
      const msg = result?.ResponseMetadata?.Error?.Message ?? result?.message ?? JSON.stringify(result).slice(0, 200);
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ error: `即梦图片生成失败（${code}）: ${msg}` }),
        { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
      );
    }

    // 异步任务模式：返回 task_id，由查询接口获取结果
    const taskId = result?.data?.task_id ?? result?.task_id ?? null;
    if (taskId) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ imageId: String(taskId), status: "pending" }),
        { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
      );
    }

    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: `未知响应格式: ${JSON.stringify(result).slice(0, 200)}` }),
      { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
    );
  } catch (err) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: `即梦图片生成失败: ${(err as Error).message}` }),
      { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
    );
  }
});

async function uploadImageToStorage(imageUrl: string): Promise<string | null> {

serve(async (req: Request): Promise<Response> => {
  if (req.method === "OPTIONS") {
    return new Response(null, { status: 204, headers: corsHeaders() });
  }

  if (req.method !== "POST") {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: "Method Not Allowed" }),
      { status: 405, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
    );
  }

  let accessKeyId = "";
  let secretAccessKey = "";
  let taskId = "";

  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    accessKeyId = (body.access_key_id as string) ?? "";
    secretAccessKey = (body.secret_access_key as string) ?? "";
    taskId = (body.task_id as string) ?? "";
  } catch {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: "Invalid request body" }),
      { status: 400, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
    );
  }

  if (!accessKeyId || !secretAccessKey) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: "缺少 Access Key ID 或 Secret Access Key" }),
      { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
    );
  }

  if (!taskId) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: "缺少 task_id 参数" }),
      { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
    );
  }

  const endpoint = "https://visual.volcengineapi.com";
  const uri = "/";
  const query = "Action=CVSync2AsyncQueryTask&Version=2022-08-31";
  const payload = JSON.stringify({
    req_key: "jimeng_t2i_v40",
    task_id: taskId,
  });

  const now = new Date();
  const xDate = now.toISOString().replace(/[:\-]|\.\d{3}/g, "").slice(0, 15) + "Z";
  const headers: Record<string, string> = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Host": "visual.volcengineapi.com",
    "X-Date": xDate,
  };

  try {
    const authorization = await buildAuthorization(
      accessKeyId,
      secretAccessKey,
      "POST",
      uri,
      query,
      headers,
      payload,
    );

    const resp = await fetch(`${endpoint}${uri}?${query}`, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        ...headers,
        "Authorization": authorization,
      },
      body: payload,
      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(30000),
    });

    const result = await resp.json();

    // 火山引擎错误码处理
    if (result.code !== 10000 && result.code !== "10000") {
      const code = result?.ResponseMetadata?.Error?.Code ?? result?.code ?? "";
      const msg = result?.ResponseMetadata?.Error?.Message ?? result?.message ?? JSON.stringify(result).slice(0, 200);
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ error: `查询失败（${code}）: ${msg}` }),
        { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
      );
    }

    // 火山引擎返回格式: data.status = "done" / "in_queue" / "generating" / "not_found" / "expired"
    const status = result?.data?.status ?? "unknown";
    const imageUrls = result?.data?.image_urls as string[] | undefined;
    const firstImageUrl = imageUrls && imageUrls.length > 0 ? imageUrls[0] : null;

    if (status === "done") {
      if (firstImageUrl) {
        const publicUrl = await uploadImageToStorage(firstImageUrl);
        return new Response(
          JSON.stringify({
            status: "completed",
            progress: 100,
            image_url: publicUrl ?? firstImageUrl,
            publicUrl: publicUrl ?? firstImageUrl,
            error: null,
          }),
          { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
        );
      }
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ status: "completed", progress: 100, error: null }),
        { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
      );
    }

    if (status === "expired" || status === "not_found") {
      const errMsg = result?.message ?? "任务已过期或不存在";
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ status: "failed", progress: 0, error: errMsg }),
        { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
      );
    }

    // in_queue / generating / pending
    const progress = status === "in_queue" ? 20 : status === "generating" ? 60 : 50;
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ status: "pending", progress, error: null }),
      { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
    );
  } catch (err) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: `查询失败: ${(err as Error).message}` }),
      { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },
    );
  }
});

    68 interface ApiSettingsDialogProps {
    69   open: boolean;
    70   onOpenChange: (open: boolean) => void;
    71   onSave?: (config: ApiConfig) => void;

    73 
    74 function emptyProviderConfig(): ModelProviderConfig {
    75   return { source: 'builtin', provider: '', apiBaseUrl: '', apiKey: '', modelName: '' };
    76 }
    77 
    78 function genId() {
    79   return Math.random().toString(36).slice(2) + Date.now().toString(36);
    80 }
    81 
    82 function emptyProfile(): CustomApiProfile {
    83   return { id: genId(), name: '', provider: 'openai', apiBaseUrl: '', apiKey: '', modelName: '', isDefault: false, extra: {} };
    84 }
    85 
    86 // 提供商默认配置映射（按模型类型区分）
    87 const PROVIDER_DEFAULTS: Record<string, { url: string; model: string }> = {
    88   openai:   { url: 'https://api.openai.com/v1',   model: 'gpt-4o-mini' },
    89   deepseek: { url: 'https://api.deepseek.com/v1', model: 'deepseek-chat' },
    90   qwen:     { url: 'https://dashscope.aliyuncs.com/compatible-mode/v1', model: 'qwen-max' },
    91   kimi:     { url: 'https://api.moonshot.cn/v1',   model: 'moonshot-v1-8k' },
    92   doubao:   { url: 'https://ark.cn-beijing.volces.com/api/v3', model: 'doubao-pro-32k' },
    93   jimeng:   { url: 'https://ark.cn-beijing.volces.com/api/v3', model: 'jimeng-t2i-v40' },
    94   kling:    { url: 'https://api.klingai.com/v1',   model: '' },
    95   vidu:     { url: 'https://api.vidu.cn',          model: 'viduq2' },
    96   sensenova:{ url: 'https://token.sensenova.cn/v1', model: 'sensenova-u1-fast' },
    97 };
    98 
    99 /** 获取某供应商在指定模型类型下的默认配置 */
   100 function getProviderDefaults(provider: string, type: keyof ModelConfig): { url: string; model: string } | undefined {
   101   const base = PROVIDER_DEFAULTS[provider];
   102   if (!base) return undefined;
   103   // 图片模型个性化默认值
   104   if (type === 'image') {
   105     if (provider === 'jimeng') return { url: 'https://ark.cn-beijing.volces.com/api/v3', model: 'jimeng-t2i-v40' };
   106     if (provider === 'vidu') return { url: 'https://api.vidu.cn', model: 'viduq2' };
   107     if (provider === 'sensenova') return { url: 'https://token.sensenova.cn/v1', model: 'sensenova-u1-fast' };
   108     if (provider === 'kling') return { url: '', model: '' };
   109   }
   110   // 视频模型个性化默认值
   111   if (type === 'video') {
   112     if (provider === 'jimeng') return { url: 'https://ark.cn-beijing.volces.com/api/v3', model: 'jimeng-video-generate-3.0' };
   113     if (provider === 'vidu') return { url: 'https://api.vidu.cn', model: '' };
   114     if (provider === 'kling') return { url: '', model: '' };
   115   }
   116   return base;
   117 }

   186 // ─── Profile Editor ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   187 interface ProfileEditorProps {
   188   profile: CustomApiProfile;
   189   options: { value: string; label: string }[];
   190   onChange: (patch: Partial<CustomApiProfile>) => void;
   191   onCancel: () => void;
   192   onConfirm: () => void;
   193   isNew: boolean;
   194   showKey: boolean;
   195   onToggleKey: () => void;
   196 }
   197 
   198 function ProfileEditor({ profile, options, onChange, onCancel, onConfirm, isNew, showKey, onToggleKey, type }: ProfileEditorProps & { type: keyof ModelConfig }) {
   199   const handleProviderChange = (newProvider: string) => {
   200     const oldDef = getProviderDefaults(profile.provider, type);
   201     const newDef = getProviderDefaults(newProvider, type);
   202     const patch: Partial<CustomApiProfile> = { provider: newProvider };
   203     // 如果地址为空或是旧提供商的默认值，则自动填充新提供商的默认值
   204     if (!profile.apiBaseUrl || (oldDef && profile.apiBaseUrl === oldDef.url)) {
   205       patch.apiBaseUrl = newDef?.url ?? '';
   206     }
   207     // 同理自动填充默认模型名
   208     if (!profile.modelName || (oldDef && profile.modelName === oldDef.model)) {
   209       patch.modelName = newDef?.model ?? '';
   210     }
   211     // 切换供应商时清空extra
   212     patch.extra = {};
   213     onChange(patch);
   214   };
   215 
   216   const provider = profile.provider;
   217   const isJimeng = provider === 'jimeng';
   218   // 固定地址的供应商不需要用户填写Base URL
   219   const fixedUrlProviders = ['vidu', 'kling', 'jimeng', 'sensenova'];
   220   const showBaseUrl = !fixedUrlProviders.includes(provider);
   221   // 图片模型中部分供应商模型名是固定的或有默认值
   222   const showModelName = type !== 'image' || (provider !== 'vidu' && provider !== 'jimeng');
   223 
   224   return (
   225     <div className="space-y-3 border border-primary/30 rounded-md p-4 bg-primary/5">
   226       <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">{isNew ? '新增 API 配置' : '编辑 API 配置'}</p>
   227       <div className="space-y-2">
   228         <Label className="text-xs">配置名称</Label>
   229         <Input
   230           placeholder="例如：我的 DeepSeek 账号"
   231           value={profile.name}
   232           onChange={(e) => onChange({ name: e.target.value })}
   233           className="h-8 text-sm"
   234         />
   235       </div>
   236       <div className="space-y-2">
   237         <Label className="text-xs">模型提供商</Label>
   238         <select
   239           value={profile.provider}
   240           onChange={(e) => handleProviderChange(e.target.value)}
   241           className="w-full h-8 px-2 text-sm rounded-md border border-input bg-background"
   242         >
   243           {options.map((opt) => (
   244             <option key={opt.value} value={opt.value}>{opt.label}</option>
   245           ))}
   246         </select>
   247       </div>
   248       {showBaseUrl && (
   249         <div className="space-y-2">
   250           <Label className="text-xs">接口基础地址</Label>

  const doSave = async (opts?: { close?: boolean }) => {
    const config: ApiConfig = {

JSON.stringify(result).slice(0, 200);\n      return new Response(\n        JSON.stringify({ error: `查询失败（${code}）: ${msg}` }),\n        { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },\n      );\n    }\n\n    // 火山引擎返回格式: data.status = "done" / "in_queue" / "generating" / "not_found" / "expired"\n    const status = result?.data?.status ?? "unknown";\n    const imageUrls = result?.data?.image_urls as string[] | undefined;\n    const firstImageUrl = imageUrls && imageUrls.length > 0 ? imageUrls[0] : null;\n\n    if (status === "done") {\n      if (firstImageUrl) {\n        const publicUrl = await uploadImageToStorage(firstImageUrl);\n        return new Response(\n          JSON.stringify({\n            status: "completed",\n            progress: 100,\n            image_url: publicUrl ?? firstImageUrl,\n            publicUrl: publicUrl ?? firstImageUrl,\n            error: null,\n          }),\n          { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },\n        );\n      }\n      return new Response(\n        JSON.stringify({ status: "completed", progress: 100, error: null }),\n        { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },\n      );\n    }\n\n    if (status === "expired" || status === "not_found") {\n      const errMsg = result?.message ?? "任务已过期或不存在";\n      return new Response(\n        JSON.stringify({ status: "failed", progress: 0, error: errMsg }),\n        { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },\n      );\n    }\n\n    // in_queue / generating / pending\n    const progress = status === "in_queue" ? 20 : status === "generating" ? 60 : 50;\n    return new Response(\n      JSON.stringify({ status: "pending", progress, error: null }),\n      { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },\n    );\n  } catch (err) {\n    return new Response(\n      JSON.stringify({ error: `查询失败: ${(err as Error).message}` }),\n      { status: 200, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...corsHeaders() } },\n    );\n  }\n});\n'}]}

"""
文本句子分割模块
功能：将文章分割为语音段落和字幕块
作者：视频生成系统
版本：1.0.0
"""

from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import List, Dict, Optional, Any
from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
import re
from datetime import datetime
import yaml
import json
import os

# ==================== 数据结构定义 ====================

@dataclass
class SubtitleBlock:
    """字幕块数据结构"""
    text: str                    # 字幕文本
    display_order: int           # 显示顺序
    start_time: float            # 开始时间（相对于段落）
    duration: float              # 显示时长
    parent_segment_id: int       # 所属语音段落ID
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        """转换为字典格式"""
        return {
            "text": self.text,
            "display_order": self.display_order,
            "start_time": round(self.start_time, 2),
            "duration": round(self.duration, 2),
            "parent_segment_id": self.parent_segment_id
        }

@dataclass
class SpeechSegment:
    """语音段落数据结构"""
    text: str                    # 段落文本
    estimated_duration: float    # 预估时长（秒）
    segment_id: int              # 段落序号
    target_words: int            # 目标字数
    subtitles: List[SubtitleBlock] = field(default_factory=list)  # 字幕块列表
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        """转换为字典格式"""
        return {
            "segment_id": self.segment_id,
            "text": self.text,
            "estimated_duration": round(self.estimated_duration, 2),
            "target_words": self.target_words,
            "subtitles": [sub.to_dict() for sub in self.subtitles]
        }

# ==================== 配置类定义 ====================

@dataclass
class SentenceTokenizerConfig:
    """句子边界消歧配置"""
    language: str = "zh"
    handle_abbreviations: bool = True
    custom_abbreviations: List[str] = field(default_factory=lambda: [
        "Dr.", "Mr.", "Ms.", "等", "etc.", "i.e.", "e.g."
    ])
    max_sentence_length: int = 200

@dataclass
class SceneSegmentationConfig:
    """场景级分割配置"""
    # 🎯 核心可配置参数
    target_seconds: float = 6.0           # 目标语音时长
    base_words_per_second: float = 3.3    # 基础语速
    speech_rate: float = 1.0              # 语速系数
    
    # 边界限制
    min_words_per_segment: int = 10
    max_words_per_segment: int = 50
    
    # 分割策略
    enforce_sentence_boundary: bool = True
    allow_single_sentence_overflow: bool = True
    
    def calculate_target_words(self) -> int:
        """计算目标字数"""
        target_words = int(self.target_seconds * self.base_words_per_second * self.speech_rate)
        return max(self.min_words_per_segment, min(target_words, self.max_words_per_segment))

@dataclass
class SubtitleSegmentationConfig:
    """字幕级分割配置"""
    min_chars_per_block: int = 8
    max_chars_per_block: int = 15
    
    # 分割优先级
    punctuation_priority: List[str] = field(default_factory=lambda: [
        "。", "！", "？", "；",  # 中文标点
        ".", "!", "?", ";",  # 英文标点
        "，", ",",  # 逗号
        "、",  # 顿号
        " ", "\n", "\t"  # 空格和换行
    ])
    
    time_calculation_method: str = "proportional"  # proportional|equal

@dataclass
class TextSegmentationConfig:
    """完整的文本分割配置"""
    sentence_tokenizer: SentenceTokenizerConfig = field(default_factory=SentenceTokenizerConfig)
    scene: SceneSegmentationConfig = field(default_factory=SceneSegmentationConfig)
    subtitle: SubtitleSegmentationConfig = field(default_factory=SubtitleSegmentationConfig)
    
    @classmethod
    def from_yaml(cls, yaml_path: str) -> 'TextSegmentationConfig':
        """从YAML文件加载配置"""
        with open(yaml_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            config_data = yaml.safe_load(f)
        return cls.from_dict(config_data)
    
    @classmethod
    def from_dict(cls, config_dict: Dict) -> 'TextSegmentationConfig':
        """从字典创建配置"""
        return cls(
            sentence_tokenizer=SentenceTokenizerConfig(**config_dict.get('sentence_tokenizer', {})),
            scene=SceneSegmentationConfig(**config_dict.get('scene', {})),
            subtitle=SubtitleSegmentationConfig(**config_dict.get('subtitle', {}))
        )
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        """转换为字典格式"""
        return {
            "sentence_tokenizer": {
                "language": self.sentence_tokenizer.language,
                "handle_abbreviations": self.sentence_tokenizer.handle_abbreviations,
                "custom_abbreviations": self.sentence_tokenizer.custom_abbreviations,
                "max_sentence_length": self.sentence_tokenizer.max_sentence_length
            },
            "scene": {
                "target_seconds": self.scene.target_seconds,
                "base_words_per_second": self.scene.base_words_per_second,
                "speech_rate": self.scene.speech_rate,
                "min_words_per_segment": self.scene.min_words_per_segment,
                "max_words_per_segment": self.scene.max_words_per_segment,
                "enforce_sentence_boundary": self.scene.enforce_sentence_boundary,
                "allow_single_sentence_overflow": self.scene.allow_single_sentence_overflow
            },
            "subtitle": {
                "min_chars_per_block": self.subtitle.min_chars_per_block,
                "max_chars_per_block": self.subtitle.max_chars_per_block,
                "punctuation_priority": self.subtitle.punctuation_priority,
                "time_calculation_method": self.subtitle.time_calculation_method
            }
        }

# ==================== 核心模块接口 ====================

class ISentenceTokenizer(ABC):
    """句子边界消歧接口"""
    @abstractmethod
    def split(self, text: str) -> List[str]:
        """将文本分割为句子列表"""
        pass

class ISceneSegmenter(ABC):
    """场景级分割接口"""
    @abstractmethod
    def segment(self, text: str) -> List[SpeechSegment]:
        """将文本分割为语音段落"""
        pass

class ISubtitleSegmenter(ABC):
    """字幕级分割接口"""
    @abstractmethod
    def segment(self, text: str, parent_duration: float, parent_id: int) -> List[SubtitleBlock]:
        """将文本分割为字幕块"""
        pass

# ==================== 具体实现类 ====================

class SentenceTokenizer(ISentenceTokenizer):
    """句子边界消歧器实现"""
    
    def __init__(self, config: SentenceTokenizerConfig):
        self.config = config
        # 编译正则表达式模式以提高性能
        self._compile_patterns()
    
    def _compile_patterns(self):
        """编译正则表达式模式"""
        # 基本句子分隔符：句号、感叹号、问号
        self.sentence_delimiters = re.compile(r'([。！？])')
        
        # 处理缩写
        abbreviations = '|'.join(re.escape(abbr) for abbr in self.config.custom_abbreviations)
        self.abbreviation_pattern = re.compile(fr'\b({abbreviations})\b')
    
    def split(self, text: str) -> List[str]:
        """
        将文本分割为句子列表
        注意：这是一个简化实现，实际需要更复杂的句子边界消歧算法
        """
        if not text or not text.strip():
            return []
        
        # 1. 预处理：合并空白字符
        text = re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', text.strip())
        
        # 2. 特殊情况处理：处理缩写
        # 这里只是简单替换，实际需要更复杂的逻辑
        placeholder = "##ABBR##"
        abbreviations_found = {}
        
        for i, abbr in enumerate(self.config.custom_abbreviations):
            if abbr in text:
                placeholder_key = f"{placeholder}{i}"
                abbreviations_found[placeholder_key] = abbr
                text = text.replace(abbr, placeholder_key)
        
        # 3. 按句子分隔符分割
        parts = self.sentence_delimiters.split(text)
        sentences = []
        current_sentence = ""
        
        for i in range(0, len(parts) - 1, 2):
            current_sentence += parts[i]
            if i + 1 < len(parts):
                delimiter = parts[i + 1]
                current_sentence += delimiter
                
                # 恢复缩写
                for key, abbr in abbreviations_found.items():
                    current_sentence = current_sentence.replace(key, abbr)
                
                sentences.append(current_sentence.strip())
                current_sentence = ""
        
        # 处理最后一部分
        if current_sentence:
            for key, abbr in abbreviations_found.items():
                current_sentence = current_sentence.replace(key, abbr)
            sentences.append(current_sentence.strip())
        
        # 4. 过滤空句子
        sentences = [s for s in sentences if s]
        
        # 5. 处理过长的句子
        result = []
        for sentence in sentences:
            if len(sentence) <= self.config.max_sentence_length:
                result.append(sentence)
            else:
                # 对过长的句子进行简单分割
                result.extend(self._split_long_sentence(sentence))
        
        return result
    
    def _split_long_sentence(self, sentence: str) -> List[str]:
        """分割过长的句子（简单实现）"""
        # 在逗号处分隔
        parts = re.split(r'[，,;；]', sentence)
        result = []
        current_part = ""
        
        for part in parts:
            if not part:
                continue
                
            if not current_part:
                current_part = part
            elif len(current_part) + len(part) + 1 <= self.config.max_sentence_length:
                current_part += "，" + part
            else:
                result.append(current_part)
                current_part = part
        
        if current_part:
            result.append(current_part)
        
        return result

class SceneSegmenter(ISceneSegmenter):
    """场景级分割器实现"""
    
    def __init__(self, config: SceneSegmentationConfig, sentence_tokenizer: ISentenceTokenizer):
        self.config = config
        self.sentence_tokenizer = sentence_tokenizer
    
    def segment(self, text: str) -> List[SpeechSegment]:
        """将文本分割为语音段落"""
        # 1. 首先分割为句子
        sentences = self.sentence_tokenizer.split(text)
        if not sentences:
            return []
        
        # 2. 计算目标字数
        target_words = self.config.calculate_target_words()
        
        # 3. 合并句子为段落
        segments = []
        current_segment = []
        current_word_count = 0
        segment_id = 0
        
        for sentence in sentences:
            sentence_word_count = len(sentence)
            
            # 如果当前段落为空，或者添加这句后不超过目标字数
            if (not current_segment or 
                current_word_count + sentence_word_count <= target_words or
                (self.config.allow_single_sentence_overflow and len(current_segment) == 0)):
                
                current_segment.append(sentence)
                current_word_count += sentence_word_count
            else:
                # 创建段落
                if current_segment:
                    segment_text = "".join(current_segment)
                    segments.append(self._create_speech_segment(
                        segment_text, segment_id, current_word_count
                    ))
                    segment_id += 1
                
                # 开始新段落
                current_segment = [sentence]
                current_word_count = sentence_word_count
        
        # 添加最后一个段落
        if current_segment:
            segment_text = "".join(current_segment)
            segments.append(self._create_speech_segment(
                segment_text, segment_id, current_word_count
            ))
        
        return segments
    
    def _create_speech_segment(self, text: str, segment_id: int, word_count: int) -> SpeechSegment:
        """创建SpeechSegment对象"""
        # 计算预估时长
        estimated_duration = word_count / (self.config.base_words_per_second * self.config.speech_rate)
        
        return SpeechSegment(
            text=text,
            estimated_duration=estimated_duration,
            segment_id=segment_id,
            target_words=word_count
        )

class SubtitleSegmenter(ISubtitleSegmenter):
    """字幕级分割器实现"""
    
    def __init__(self, config: SubtitleSegmentationConfig, sentence_tokenizer: ISentenceTokenizer):
        self.config = config
        self.sentence_tokenizer = sentence_tokenizer
    
    def segment(self, text: str, parent_duration: float, parent_id: int) -> List[SubtitleBlock]:
        """将文本分割为字幕块"""
        # 1. 分割为句子
        sentences = self.sentence_tokenizer.split(text)
        if not sentences:
            return []
        
        # 2. 进一步分割每个句子
        all_blocks = []
        for sentence in sentences:
            blocks = self._split_sentence_into_blocks(sentence)
            all_blocks.extend(blocks)
        
        # 3. 计算时间戳
        blocks_with_time = self._calculate_timestamps(all_blocks, parent_duration, parent_id)
        
        return blocks_with_time
    
    def _split_sentence_into_blocks(self, sentence: str) -> List[str]:
        """将单个句子分割为字幕块"""
        blocks = []
        current_block = ""
        
        # 按字符遍历句子
        for char in sentence:
            # 如果遇到分割符，并且当前块不为空
            if char in self.config.punctuation_priority and current_block:
                # 添加分隔符到当前块
                current_block += char
                
                # 检查当前块长度
                if len(current_block) >= self.config.min_chars_per_block:
                    blocks.append(current_block)
                    current_block = ""
                else:
                    # 如果块太小，暂时保留
                    pass
            else:
                current_block += char
            
            # 如果当前块达到最大长度，强制分割
            if len(current_block) >= self.config.max_chars_per_block:
                # 尝试在合适位置分割
                split_pos = self._find_split_position(current_block)
                if split_pos > 0:
                    blocks.append(current_block[:split_pos])
                    current_block = current_block[split_pos:]
                else:
                    # 没有合适的分割点，强制在最大长度处分割
                    blocks.append(current_block)
                    current_block = ""
        
        # 处理剩余的字符
        if current_block:
            # 如果最后一块太小，合并到前一块
            if len(current_block) < self.config.min_chars_per_block and blocks:
                last_block = blocks.pop()
                blocks.append(last_block + current_block)
            else:
                blocks.append(current_block)
        
        return blocks
    
    def _find_split_position(self, text: str) -> int:
        """找到合适的分割位置"""
        # 优先在标点处分隔
        for i in range(len(text) - 1, -1, -1):
            if text[i] in self.config.punctuation_priority:
                return i + 1  # 在标点后分割
        
        # 其次在空格处分隔
        for i in range(len(text) - 1, -1, -1):
            if text[i] in [' ', '　', '\t']:
                return i + 1
        
        # 没有合适的分割点
        return -1
    
    def _calculate_timestamps(self, blocks: List[str], total_duration: float, parent_id: int) -> List[SubtitleBlock]:
        """计算每个字幕块的时间戳"""
        if not blocks:
            return []
        
        if self.config.time_calculation_method == "equal":
            # 平均分配时间
            block_duration = total_duration / len(blocks)
            subtitle_blocks = []
            
            for i, block_text in enumerate(blocks):
                subtitle_block = SubtitleBlock(
                    text=block_text,
                    display_order=i,
                    start_time=i * block_duration,
                    duration=block_duration,
                    parent_segment_id=parent_id
                )
                subtitle_blocks.append(subtitle_block)
        
        else:  # proportional
            # 按字数比例分配时间
            total_chars = sum(len(block) for block in blocks)
            subtitle_blocks = []
            current_time = 0.0
            
            for i, block_text in enumerate(blocks):
                block_duration = (len(block_text) / total_chars) * total_duration
                
                subtitle_block = SubtitleBlock(
                    text=block_text,
                    display_order=i,
                    start_time=current_time,
                    duration=block_duration,
                    parent_segment_id=parent_id
                )
                subtitle_blocks.append(subtitle_block)
                
                current_time += block_duration
        
        return subtitle_blocks

# ==================== 主模块 ====================

class TextSegmentationModule:
    """文本句子分割主模块"""
    
    def __init__(self, config: Optional[TextSegmentationConfig] = None):
        """初始化模块"""
        self.config = config or TextSegmentationConfig()
        self.sentence_tokenizer = SentenceTokenizer(self.config.sentence_tokenizer)
        self.scene_segmenter = SceneSegmenter(self.config.scene, self.sentence_tokenizer)
        self.subtitle_segmenter = SubtitleSegmenter(self.config.subtitle, self.sentence_tokenizer)
    
    def process(self, text: str) -> Dict:
        """
        完整处理文本分割流程
        返回结构化的分割结果
        """
        if not text or not text.strip():
            raise ValueError("输入文本不能为空")
        
        try:
            # 1. 场景级分割
            speech_segments = self.scene_segmenter.segment(text)
            
            # 2. 为每个语音段落生成字幕
            for segment in speech_segments:
                subtitle_blocks = self.subtitle_segmenter.segment(
                    text=segment.text,
                    parent_duration=segment.estimated_duration,
                    parent_id=segment.segment_id
                )
                segment.subtitles = subtitle_blocks
            
            # 3. 计算总体统计
            total_duration = sum(s.estimated_duration for s in speech_segments)
            total_words = sum(len(s.text) for s in speech_segments)
            
            # 4. 返回结构化结果
            return {
                "speech_segments": [s.to_dict() for s in speech_segments],
                "total_duration": round(total_duration, 2),
                "total_words": total_words,
                "segment_count": len(speech_segments),
                "config": self.config.to_dict()
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            # 记录错误并重新抛出
            error_msg = f"文本分割处理失败: {str(e)}"
            raise RuntimeError(error_msg) from e
    
    def update_config(self, config: TextSegmentationConfig):
        """更新配置"""
        self.config = config
        self.sentence_tokenizer = SentenceTokenizer(self.config.sentence_tokenizer)
        self.scene_segmenter = SceneSegmenter(self.config.scene, self.sentence_tokenizer)
        self.subtitle_segmenter = SubtitleSegmenter(self.config.subtitle, self.sentence_tokenizer)
    
    def get_config_summary(self) -> Dict:
        """获取配置摘要"""
        return {
            "scene_config": {
                "target_seconds": self.config.scene.target_seconds,
                "speech_rate": self.config.scene.speech_rate,
                "target_words": self.config.scene.calculate_target_words()
            },
            "subtitle_config": {
                "min_chars_per_block": self.config.subtitle.min_chars_per_block,
                "max_chars_per_block": self.config.subtitle.max_chars_per_block
            }
        }

# ==================== 工具函数 ====================

def save_result_to_json(result: Dict, filepath: str):
    """将结果保存为JSON文件"""
    with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        json.dump(result, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)

def load_config_from_file(filepath: str) -> TextSegmentationConfig:
    """从文件加载配置（支持YAML和JSON）"""
    if filepath.endswith('.yaml') or filepath.endswith('.yml'):
        return TextSegmentationConfig.from_yaml(filepath)
    elif filepath.endswith('.json'):
        with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            config_dict = json.load(f)
        return TextSegmentationConfig.from_dict(config_dict)
    else:
        raise ValueError("不支持的文件格式，请使用.yaml或.json文件")

# ==================== 使用示例 ====================

def main():
    """使用示例"""
    print("=== 文本句子分割模块示例 ===\n")
    
    # 示例文本
    example_text = """
    人工智能是当今科技领域最重要的技术之一。它正在改变我们的生活和工作方式。
    机器学习、深度学习等技术让计算机能够像人类一样学习和思考。未来，AI将在医疗、教育、交通等各个领域发挥更大作用。
    我们需要认真思考AI的伦理问题，确保技术发展符合人类利益。
    """
    
    try:
        # 1. 创建默认配置
        print("1. 创建默认配置...")
        config = TextSegmentationConfig()
        
        # 2. 初始化模块
        print("2. 初始化分割模块...")
        module = TextSegmentationModule(config)
        
        # 3. 处理文本
        print("3. 处理文本...")
        result = module.process(example_text)
        
        # 4. 显示结果
        print(f"\n4. 分割结果：")
        print(f"   总段落数：{result['segment_count']}")
        print(f"   总时长：{result['total_duration']}秒")
        print(f"   总字数：{result['total_words']}")
        
        print(f"\n5. 详细分段：")
        for i, segment in enumerate(result['speech_segments']):
            print(f"   段落 {i+1}（{segment['estimated_duration']}秒，{segment['target_words']}字）：")
            print(f"     {segment['text'][:50]}...")
            print(f"     字幕块数：{len(segment['subtitles'])}")
            for j, subtitle in enumerate(segment['subtitles']):
                print(f"      字幕 {j+1}: {subtitle['text']} ({subtitle['duration']}秒)")
            print()
        
        # 5. 保存结果
        save_result_to_json(result, "segmentation_result.json")
        print(f"6. 结果已保存到: segmentation_result.json")
        
        # 6. 显示配置
        config_summary = module.get_config_summary()
        print(f"\n7. 当前配置：")
        print(f"   目标时长：{config_summary['scene_config']['target_seconds']}秒")
        print(f"   语速系数：{config_summary['scene_config']['speech_rate']}")
        print(f"   目标字数：{config_summary['scene_config']['target_words']}字")
        print(f"   字幕范围：{config_summary['subtitle_config']['min_chars_per_block']}-{config_summary['subtitle_config']['max_chars_per_block']}字")
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"处理失败: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# 需求文档：AI字幕智能分词与无标点断行系统

## 🚨 System Prompt (给 AI Vibe Coding 的核心指令)
> **复制这一段给 AI 作为开场白**

```markdown
# Role
你是一名拥有 10 年经验的音视频客户端架构师，专精于字幕渲染引擎（Subtitle Rendering Engine）和自然语言处理（NLP）。

# Goal
实现一个 Python 函数，将任意长文本转化为短视频字幕数组。
**硬性指标**：每行 ≤ 12 个汉字，输出结果 **严禁包含任何标点符号**（，。！？；、等）。

# Strict Rules (铁律)
1.  **NO SUBSTRING (严禁机械截断)**：绝对禁止使用 `text[0:12]` 或 `slice()`。必须将句子视为由词语组成的链条，而不是字符序列。
2.  **Punctuation as Signposts (标点仅作路标)**：逗号、句号等标点**仅用于判断在哪里断行**，绝不能出现在最终输出数组中。
3.  **Semantic Integrity (语意完整性)**：
    - 禁止将“主语+谓语”拆散。
    - 禁止将定语（如“妈妈做的”）与中心语（如“红烧肉”）强行剥离。
    - 关联词（因为/所以）需保持在同一行。
4.  **Token First (分词优先)**：必须使用 `jieba` 分词。专有名词（如“中华人民共和国”）是不可分割的原子单位。

# Execution Steps (严格执行顺序)
1.  **Split by Punctuation**: 先用正则按标点切割，得到逻辑段落。
2.  **Tokenize**: 对每个段落使用 `jieba.lcut()` 分词。
3.  **Accumulate (Greedy)**: 从左往右累加词的长度。
4.  **Break Line**: 当加入下一个词会超过 12 字时，**立刻停止**并在此处断行。
5.  **Sanitize**: 在存入数组前，彻底清除该行残留的标点。
6.  **Return**: 输出干净的字符串数组。

# Anti-patterns (反面教材 - 绝对禁止)
- ❌ 输入 "我喜欢吃妈妈做的红烧肉" -> 输出 ["我喜欢吃妈妈做的", "红烧肉"] 
  (错误：将定语“妈妈做的”剥离，语意断裂)
- ❌ 输入 "你好，世界" -> 输出 ["你好，", "世界"]
  (错误：保留了逗号)
```

---

## 1. 需求概述 (Overview)
为了确保短视频字幕的阅读效率与视觉美感，需对长文本进行智能化重排。系统需基于**中文分词（CWS）**与**语义边界检测**，将文本拆分为单行不超过 12 字的数组，并自动剔除所有逻辑性标点符号。

## 2. 核心约束 (Core Constraints)
| 约束项 | 规则定义 |
| :--- | :--- |
| **最大行宽** | $\le$ 12 个汉字（含数字/英文，按 2:1 折算）。 |
| **输出内容** | **纯文本**。严禁出现逗号、句号、感叹号、顿号、分号。 |
| **最小粒度** | **词语（Token）**。例如“陆家嘴”不可拆为“陆/家/嘴”。 |
| **断行依据** | 标点符号（逻辑断点） > 分词边界（语义断点）。 |

## 3. 算法逻辑 (Algorithm Specification)

### 3.1 逻辑流程图
1.  **输入**：`“今天天气真不错，我们去公园散步吧！记得带上你的相机。”`
2.  **逻辑分段**：`["今天天气真不错，", "我们去公园散步吧！", "记得带上你的相机。"]` （利用标点）
3.  **分词处理**：`["今天", "天气", "真", "不错", ",", "我们", "去", "公园", "散步", "吧", "!"]`
4.  **贪心组装**：
    *   当前行：`["今天", "天气", "真", "不错"]` (8字) -> 尝试加`","` -> 忽略标点 -> 尝试加`"我们"` -> 超过12字 -> **断行**。
    *   新行：`["我们", "去", "公园", "散步", "吧"]` -> 尝试加`"!"` -> 忽略 -> **断行**。
5.  **清洗输出**：`["今天天气真不错", "我们去公园散步吧", "记得带上你的相机"]`

### 3.2 伪代码实现 (Python)
```
import re
import jieba
from stopwords import STOP_WORDS 

    MAX_LINE_LENGTH = 12

    def split_text(self, text: str) -> list[str]:
        """
        将长文本拆分为无标点的字幕数组
        """
        # 1. 按标点符号进行粗分句 (保留标点用于逻辑判断)
        # 注意：这里使用捕获组，确保标点成为数组的一部分，用于断句参考
        segments = re.split(r'([，。！？；、])', text)

        result_subtitles = []

        for segment in segments:
            if not segment or segment in STOP_WORDS:
                continue

            # 2. 分词 (Tokenization)
            tokens = jieba.lcut(segment)

            current_line = ""

            # 3. 贪心算法填充 (Greedy Accumulation)
            for token in tokens:
                # 跳过纯标点符号（因为它们只是路标，不是内容）
                if token in '，。！？；、':
                    continue

                if len(current_line) + len(token) <= self.MAX_LINE_LENGTH:
                    current_line += token
                else:
                    if current_line:
                        # 4. 清洗并输出
                        cleaned_line = self._clean_punctuation(current_line)
                        result_subtitles.append(cleaned_line)

                    # 处理超长Token（极罕见）
                    if len(token) > self.MAX_LINE_LENGTH:
                        result_subtitles.extend(self._force_split_token(token))
                        current_line = ""
                    else:
                        current_line = token

            # 处理循环结束后的剩余部分
            if current_line:
                cleaned_line = self._clean_punctuation(current_line)
                result_subtitles.append(cleaned_line)

        return result_subtitles

    def _clean_punctuation(self, text: str) -> str:
        """移除所有逻辑性中文标点符号"""
        pattern = r'[，。！？；、,.!?;:\s]'
        return re.sub(pattern, '', text)

    def _force_split_token(self, token: str) -> list[str]:
        """处理超过12字的单个Token（兜底逻辑）"""
        chunks = [token[i:i+self.MAX_LINE_LENGTH] for i in range(0, len(token), self.MAX_LINE_LENGTH)]
        return [self._clean_punctuation(c) for c in chunks]
```

## 4. 验收标准 (Acceptance Criteria)

### 4.1 正常场景（正例）
| ID | 输入示例 | 期望输出 (Correct) |
| :--- | :--- | :--- |
| AC-01 | `今天天气真不错，我们去公园散步吧！` | `["今天天气真不错", "我们去公园散步吧"]` |
| AC-02 | `中华人民共和国成立于1949年。` | `["中华人民共和国", "成立于1949年"]` |

### 4.2 反例场景（Anti-patterns / 严禁行为）
**核心原则：严禁语意割裂与机械截断。**

| ID | 输入示例 | ❌ **错误输出 (Forbidden)** | ✅ **正确输出 (Required)** | **错误原因分析** |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |
| **AC-03**<br>(动宾结构) | `我喜欢吃妈妈做的红烧肉` | `["我喜欢吃妈妈做的", "红烧肉"]` | `["我喜欢吃", "妈妈做的红烧肉"]` | **错误**：将“妈妈做的”这个定语强行剥离，导致上句语意不完整。<br>**正确**：保证“红烧肉”作为宾语的完整性。 |
| **AC-04**<br>(专有名词) | `上海浦东新区陆家嘴` | `["上海浦东新区陆", "家嘴"]` | `["上海浦东新区", "陆家嘴"]` | **错误**：将“陆家嘴”这个地名切开，属于机械截断。<br>**正确**：分词库应识别出这是一个整体。 |
| **AC-05**<br>(助词粘连) | `这是一只可爱的小猫` | `["这是一只可爱的", "小猫"]` | `["这是一只", "可爱的小猫"]` | **错误**：助词“的”被留在了行尾，导致阅读节奏拖沓。<br>**正确**：助词应跟随其修饰的词语。 |
| **AC-06**<br>(标点残留) | `你好，世界！` | `["你好，", "世界！"]` | `["你好", "世界"]` | **错误**：保留了标点符号。<br>**正确**：输出必须是纯文本。 |
| **AC-07**<br>(主谓分离) | `会议因为暴雨不得不取消` | `["会议因为暴雨不得", "不取消"]` | `["会议因为暴雨", "不得不取消"]` | **错误**：将“不得不”这个副词组拆散。<br>**正确**：关联词需保持在同一行内。 |

---

### 💡 给 AI 的最后调试建议
如果 AI 生成的代码在 **AC-03** 上还是出错（即仍然输出 `["我喜欢吃妈妈做的", "红烧肉"]`），请立即告诉 AI：
> **“你的算法逻辑错了。你在判断长度时，不应该只看字符数，还要看语意。‘妈妈做的’是修饰语，不能和中心语分开。请调整你的贪心算法，确保修饰语和被修饰词在同一行，即使这意味着上一行字数少一点。”**

import { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest';
import { segmentTextByCount, segmentTextBySemantics, segmentSubtitleText, buildSubtitleTimeline, getTextWidth } from './segment';

describe('segmentTextBySemantics', () => {
  it('should return single segment for short text', () => {
    expect(segmentTextBySemantics('你好')).toEqual(['你好']);
  });

  it('should split by strong punctuation (period)', () => {
    // Use maxLength=30 to force splitting at sentence boundaries
    const text = '春天悄悄地来到了人间。大地回暖，万物复苏。蝴蝶在花丛中翩翩起舞。鸟儿在歌唱。';
    const result = segmentTextBySemantics(text, 30, 15);
    expect(result.length).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(2);
    expect(result[0]).toContain('春天');
    // First segment should end with a strong punctuation
    expect(/[。！？]/.test(result[0].slice(-1))).toBe(true);
  });

  it('should respect maxLength and merge short trailing segments', () => {
    const text = '第一段文字内容。第二段文字内容。第三段。';
    const result = segmentTextBySemantics(text, 50, 20);
    expect(result.length).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(1);
    // No segment should exceed maxLength
    result.forEach((seg) => expect(seg.length).toBeLessThanOrEqual(50));
  });
});

describe('segmentTextByCount', () => {
  it('should return single segment for count <= 1', () => {
    expect(segmentTextByCount('你好世界', 1)).toEqual(['你好世界']);
  });

  it('should return single segment for short text', () => {
    expect(segmentTextByCount('你好', 4)).toEqual(['你好']);
  });

  it('should split into specified count segments', () => {
    // Long enough text (over 60 chars for count=4) to force splitting
    const text = '第一段内容描述了春天的景象。第二段内容讲述了夏天的故事。第三段内容描绘了秋天的画面。第四段内容记录了冬天的情景。这是一段额外的文字，用来确保总字数超过分割阈值。';
    const result = segmentTextByCount(text, 4);
    expect(result.length).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(2);
    expect(result.length).toBeLessThanOrEqual(4);
  });

  it('should merge trailing short segments', () => {
    const text = '这是一段很长的文字，需要被分成多段来测试分段函数是否正确工作。春天来了，万物复苏，花开满园，蝴蝶飞舞，鸟儿歌唱。';
    const result = segmentTextByCount(text, 8);
    expect(result.length).toBeLessThanOrEqual(8);
    expect(result.length).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(1);
  });
});

describe('getTextWidth', () => {
  it('should count Chinese chars as 1', () => {
    expect(getTextWidth('你好')).toBe(2);
    expect(getTextWidth('中华人民共和国')).toBe(7);
  });

  it('should count English/numbers as 0.5', () => {
    expect(getTextWidth('hello')).toBe(2.5);
    expect(getTextWidth('1949')).toBe(2);
  });

  it('should handle mixed text', () => {
    expect(getTextWidth('成立于1949年')).toBe(6); // 3中文 + 4数字*0.5 = 3+2
    expect(getTextWidth('hello世界')).toBe(4.5); // 5英文*0.5 + 2中文 = 2.5+2
  });
});

describe('segmentSubtitleText', () => {
  it('should return single segment for short text', () => {
    expect(segmentSubtitleText('你好世界')).toEqual(['你好世界']);
  });

  it('should remove all punctuation from output', () => {
    const text = '春天来了。花儿开了。蝴蝶在飞舞。';
    const result = segmentSubtitleText(text);
    result.forEach((line) => {
      expect(line).not.toMatch(/[，。！？；、,.!?;:\s]/);
    });
    expect(result.join('')).toBe('春天来了花儿开了蝴蝶在飞舞');
  });

  it('should keep each line within 12 char width', () => {
    const text = '今天天气真好啊，阳光明娚，万里无云，非常适合出去走走活动活动筋骨呢';
    const result = segmentSubtitleText(text);
    result.forEach((line) => {
      expect(getTextWidth(line)).toBeLessThanOrEqual(12);
    });
  });

  it('should not split words across lines (token-based)', () => {
    const text = '我喜欢吃妈妈做的红烧肉';
    const result = segmentSubtitleText(text);
    result.forEach((line) => {
      expect(getTextWidth(line)).toBeLessThanOrEqual(12);
    });
    const joined = result.join('');
    expect(joined).toContain('红烧肉');
    let foundIntact = false;
    for (const line of result) {
      if (line.includes('红烧肉')) foundIntact = true;
    }
    expect(foundIntact).toBe(true);
  });

  it('should split long sentence without punctuation by tokens', () => {
    const text = '春天悄悄地来到了人间大地回暖万物复苏蝴蝶在花丛中美丽地跳跳起舞';
    const result = segmentSubtitleText(text);
    result.forEach((line) => {
      expect(getTextWidth(line)).toBeLessThanOrEqual(12);
    });
    expect(result.length).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(2);
  });

  it('should handle English words with 2:1 ratio', () => {
    const text = 'hello world this is test 今天天气';
    const result = segmentSubtitleText(text);
    result.forEach((line) => {
      expect(getTextWidth(line)).toBeLessThanOrEqual(12);
    });
  });

  it('should split by comma and 顿号 punctuation', () => {
    const text = '苹果，香蕉，橙子，葡萄和西瓜';
    const result = segmentSubtitleText(text);
    result.forEach((line) => {
      expect(getTextWidth(line)).toBeLessThanOrEqual(12);
    });
    result.forEach((line) => {
      expect(line).not.toMatch(/[，。！？；、,.!?;:\s]/);
    });
  });

  it('should handle empty text', () => {
    expect(segmentSubtitleText('')).toEqual([]);
    expect(segmentSubtitleText('   ')).toEqual([]);
  });
});

describe('buildSubtitleTimeline', () => {
  it('should build timeline with correct durations', () => {
    const text = '春天来了。花儿开了。';
    const result = buildSubtitleTimeline(text, 10);
    expect(result.length).toBe(2);
    expect(result[0].startTime).toBe(0);
    expect(result[1].endTime).toBeCloseTo(10, 1);
    expect(result[0].endTime).toBeCloseTo((5 / 10) * 10, 1);
    // charTimings should exist and be proportional
    expect(result[0].charTimings.length).toBeGreaterThan(0);
    expect(result[0].charTimings[result[0].charTimings.length - 1]).toBeCloseTo(result[0].endTime, 1);
  });

  it('should handle single line', () => {
    const text = '你好';
    const result = buildSubtitleTimeline(text, 5);
    expect(result.length).toBe(1);
    expect(result[0].startTime).toBe(0);
    expect(result[0].endTime).toBe(5);
    expect(result[0].charTimings.length).toBe(2);
  });

  it('should handle empty text', () => {
    expect(buildSubtitleTimeline('', 10)).toEqual([]);
  });
});

import { Segment, useDefault } from 'segmentit';

/** 全局 segmentit 分词实例（懒加载） */
let _segmentit: InstanceType<typeof Segment> | null = null;
function getSegmenter(): InstanceType<typeof Segment> {
  if (!_segmentit) {
    _segmentit = new Segment();
    useDefault(_segmentit);
  }
  return _segmentit;
}

/**
 * 计算文本显示宽度（中文字符=1，英文/数字按2:1折算=0.5）
 */
export function getTextWidth(text: string): number {
  let width = 0;
  for (const ch of text) {
    if (/[\u4e00-\u9fa5\u3000-\u303f\uff00-\uffef]/.test(ch)) {
      width += 1; // 中文及中文标点
    } else if (/[a-zA-Z0-9]/.test(ch)) {
      width += 0.5; // 英文/数字
    } else {
      width += 1; // 其他字符按1计
    }
  }
  return width;
}

/**
 * 中文文案语义断句策略
 *
 * 核心原则：
 * 1. 强语义标点优先（句号、问号、感叹号）—— 一个完整的语义单元不应被截断
 * 2. 次语义标点辅助（分号）—— 适合作为次级断句点
 * 3. 弱标点（逗号、顿号）—— 仅作为最后回退的断句点，避免在逗号处生硬截断
 * 4. 字数控制：每段理想长度 40~120 字，最短不低于 15 字，最长不超过 150 字
 *    - 太短（<15字）会导致图片缺乏足够上下文来生成高质量画面
 *    - 太长（>150字）会导致单张图片承载过多语义，生图效果模糊
 * 5. 合并过短片段：断句后若末尾片段过短，优先向前合并而非单独成段
 */

/** 强语义结束标点（句子级） */
const STRONG_ENDERS = /[。！？]/;
/** 次语义结束标点（分句级） */
const MEDIUM_ENDERS = /[；]/;
/** 弱语义分隔标点（词组/短语级，仅作回退；包含破折号单字符 U+2014） */
const WEAK_ENDERS = /[，、\u2014]/;

/**
 * 按语义断句将文案分段
 * @param text 原始文案
 * @param maxLength 每段最大字符数（默认120）
 * @param minLength 每段最小字符数（默认40），用于合并时参考
 */
export function segmentTextBySemantics(text: string, maxLength = 120, minLength = 40): string[] {
  const trimmed = text.trim();
  if (!trimmed) return [];
  // Guard: ensure minLength does not exceed maxLength
  const effectiveMin = Math.min(minLength, maxLength);
  if (trimmed.length <= maxLength) return [trimmed];

  const segments: string[] = [];
  let current = '';
  const chars = trimmed.split('');

  for (let i = 0; i < chars.length; i++) {
    const ch = chars[i];
    current += ch;

    // 1. 强语义标点断句：只要当前长度 >= effectiveMin*0.5（>=20字），即可断句
    if (STRONG_ENDERS.test(ch) && current.length >= effectiveMin * 0.5) {
      segments.push(current.trim());
      current = '';
      continue;
    }

    // 2. 次语义标点断句：当前长度 >= effectiveMin 时，在分号处断句
    if (MEDIUM_ENDERS.test(ch) && current.length >= effectiveMin) {
      segments.push(current.trim());
      current = '';
      continue;
    }

    // 3. 强制断句：超过最大长度时，优先保证语义完整
    if (current.length >= maxLength) {
      let splitIndex = current.length;
      // 优先回退到强语义标点
      for (let j = current.length - 1; j >= Math.max(0, current.length - 30); j--) {
        if (STRONG_ENDERS.test(current[j]) || MEDIUM_ENDERS.test(current[j])) {
          splitIndex = j + 1;
          break;
        }
      }
      if (splitIndex !== current.length) {
        // 在强/次标点处截断，语义完整
        segments.push(current.slice(0, splitIndex).trim());
        current = current.slice(splitIndex).trim();
      } else {
        // 当前段内无强/次标点，宁可超限也要把完整句子保留在同一段
        // 继续向后读取到下一个强语义标点（或文本末尾）
        let found = false;
        for (let k = i + 1; k < chars.length; k++) {
          if (STRONG_ENDERS.test(chars[k])) {
            current += chars.slice(i + 1, k + 1).join('');
            i = k;
            segments.push(current.trim());
            current = '';
            found = true;
            break;
          }
        }
        if (!found) {
          // 读到末尾也没有强标点，剩余全部合并为一段
          current += chars.slice(i + 1).join('');
          i = chars.length; // 结束循环
          segments.push(current.trim());
          current = '';
        }
      }
    }
  }

  if (current.trim()) {
    segments.push(current.trim());
  }

  // 4. 合并末尾过短片段（< effectiveMin * 0.75，即默认 <30字）
  while (segments.length >= 2 && segments[segments.length - 1].length < effectiveMin * 0.75) {
    const last = segments.pop()!;
    segments[segments.length - 1] = segments[segments.length - 1] + last;
  }

  return segments;
}

/**
 * 将文案按指定数量均匀分段，尽量在语义标点处切分
 * @param text 原始文案
 * @param count 目标段数
 * @returns 分段后的文案数组
 */
export function segmentTextByCount(text: string, count: number): string[] {
  const trimmed = text.trim();
  if (!trimmed) return [];
  if (count <= 1) return [trimmed];
  if (trimmed.length <= count * 15) return [trimmed];

  const chars = trimmed.split('');
  const targetLen = Math.ceil(chars.length / count);
  const segments: string[] = [];
  let current = '';

  for (let i = 0; i < chars.length; i++) {
    const ch = chars[i];
    current += ch;

    const isNearTarget = current.length >= targetLen * 0.7;
    const isOverTarget = current.length >= targetLen;

    // 优先在强语义标点处断句
    if (isNearTarget && STRONG_ENDERS.test(ch)) {
      segments.push(current.trim());
      current = '';
      continue;
    }

    // 次优先在分号处断句
    if (isNearTarget && MEDIUM_ENDERS.test(ch)) {
      segments.push(current.trim());
      current = '';
      continue;
    }

    // 超过目标长度时，优先保证语义完整
    if (isOverTarget) {
      let splitIndex = current.length;
      for (let j = current.length - 1; j >= Math.max(0, current.length - 30); j--) {
        if (STRONG_ENDERS.test(current[j]) || MEDIUM_ENDERS.test(current[j])) {
          splitIndex = j + 1;
          break;
        }
      }
      if (splitIndex !== current.length) {
        segments.push(current.slice(0, splitIndex).trim());
        current = current.slice(splitIndex).trim();
      } else {
        // 当前段内无强/次标点，宁可超限也要保留完整句子
        let found = false;
        for (let k = i + 1; k < chars.length; k++) {
          if (STRONG_ENDERS.test(chars[k])) {
            current += chars.slice(i + 1, k + 1).join('');
            i = k;
            segments.push(current.trim());
            current = '';
            found = true;
            break;
          }
        }
        if (!found) {
          current += chars.slice(i + 1).join('');
          i = chars.length;
          segments.push(current.trim());
          current = '';
        }
      }
    }
  }

  if (current.trim()) {
    segments.push(current.trim());
  }

  // 合并末尾过短片段（< targetLen * 0.5）
  while (segments.length > count && segments.length >= 2) {
    const last = segments.pop()!;
    segments[segments.length - 1] = segments[segments.length - 1] + last;
  }

  return segments;
}

const MAX_SUBTITLE_WIDTH = 12;
/** 需要清洗掉的所有中文逻辑标点 */
const ALL_PUNCTUATION = /[，。！？；、,.!?;:\s]/g;

/** 移除所有逻辑性标点符号 */
function cleanPunctuation(text: string): string {
  return text.replace(ALL_PUNCTUATION, '');
}

/**
 * 强制截断超长 token（按最大行宽切割，并清洗标点）
 */
function forceSplitToken(token: string): string[] {
  const parts: string[] = [];
  let current = '';
  let currentWidth = 0;

  for (const ch of token) {
    const w = /[a-zA-Z0-9]/.test(ch) ? 0.5 : 1;
    if (currentWidth + w > MAX_SUBTITLE_WIDTH && current) {
      parts.push(cleanPunctuation(current));
      current = ch;
      currentWidth = w;
    } else {
      current += ch;
      currentWidth += w;
    }
  }
  if (current) parts.push(cleanPunctuation(current));
  return parts.filter((p) => p.length > 0);
}

/**
 * 字幕文字分断逻辑（基于分词的贪心算法 v2）
 *
 * 核心原则：
 * 1. 按所有中文标点（，。！？；、）粗分句，保留标点用于逻辑判断
 * 2. 对每句进行中文分词（segmentit），词语为最小单位
 * 3. 贪心填充时跳过纯标点 token，按显示宽度判断是否加入当前行
 * 4. 英文/数字按 2:1 折算（即 1 个英文字母/数字 = 0.5 个中文字符宽度）
 * 5. 若单个词汇超过 12 字宽，强制截断并清洗标点
 * 6. 每行最终输出前彻底清除所有逻辑性标点，输出纯文本
 * 7. 末尾过短片段（< 2 字宽）向前合并
 */
export function segmentSubtitleText(text: string): string[] {
  const trimmed = text.trim();
  if (!trimmed) return [];

  // 1. 按所有中文标点粗分句（包括逗号、顿号），保留标点
  const rawSegments = trimmed.split(/([，。！？；、])/);
  const segments: string[] = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < rawSegments.length; i++) {
    const s = rawSegments[i];
    if (!s) continue;
    // 若当前是标点符号，合并到前一段末尾
    if (/^[，。！？；、]$/.test(s) && segments.length > 0) {
      segments[segments.length - 1] += s;
    } else {
      segments.push(s);
    }
  }

  const result: string[] = [];
  const segmenter = getSegmenter();

  for (const segment of segments) {
    if (!segment.trim()) continue;

    // 整段（含标点）去除标点后 <= 12 字宽，直接作为一行
    const cleanedSegment = cleanPunctuation(segment);
    if (cleanedSegment.length > 0 && getTextWidth(cleanedSegment) <= MAX_SUBTITLE_WIDTH) {
      result.push(cleanedSegment);
      continue;
    }

    // 2. 分词
    const rawTokens = segmenter.doSegment(segment).map((r) => r.w);

    let currentLine = '';
    let currentWidth = 0;

    for (const token of rawTokens) {
      // 跳过纯标点 token（它们只是路标，不是内容）
      if (/^[，。！？；、]$/.test(token)) continue;

      const tokenWidth = getTextWidth(token);

      // 单 token 超长：强制截断
      if (tokenWidth > MAX_SUBTITLE_WIDTH) {
        if (currentLine) {
          result.push(cleanPunctuation(currentLine));
          currentLine = '';
          currentWidth = 0;
        }
        const forcedParts = forceSplitToken(token);
        for (let i = 0; i < forcedParts.length; i++) {
          if (i === forcedParts.length - 1) {
            currentLine = forcedParts[i];
            currentWidth = getTextWidth(forcedParts[i]);
          } else {
            result.push(forcedParts[i]);
          }
        }
        continue;
      }

      // 尝试加入当前行
      if (currentWidth + tokenWidth <= MAX_SUBTITLE_WIDTH) {
        currentLine += token;
        currentWidth += tokenWidth;
      } else {
        // 当前行已满，清洗标点后保存，开始新行
        if (currentLine) result.push(cleanPunctuation(currentLine));
        currentLine = token;
        currentWidth = tokenWidth;
      }
    }

    if (currentLine) {
      const cleaned = cleanPunctuation(currentLine);
      if (cleaned) result.push(cleaned);
    }
  }

  // 合并末尾过短片段（< 3 字宽）到前一段，确保合并后不超过 14 字宽
  for (let i = result.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
    if (getTextWidth(result[i]) < 3 && getTextWidth(result[i - 1]) + getTextWidth(result[i]) <= MAX_SUBTITLE_WIDTH + 2) {
      result[i - 1] += result[i];
      result.splice(i, 1);
    }
  }

  // 最终后处理：确保每行至少 3 个字符，过短则向前/向后合并
  for (let i = result.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
    if (result[i].length < 3) {
      result[i - 1] += result[i];
      result.splice(i, 1);
    }
  }
  // 首行过短则向后合并
  if (result.length >= 2 && result[0].length < 3) {
    result[1] = result[0] + result[1];
    result.splice(0, 1);
  }

  return result;
}

export interface SubtitleTimelineItem {
  text: string;
  startTime: number;
  endTime: number;
  /** 每个字符的结束时间（秒，相对 startTime） */
  charTimings: number[];
}

/**
 * 构建与语音时长同步的字幕时间线
 * @param text 原始文案
 * @param totalDuration 语音总时长（秒）
 * @returns 带时间段和逐字时间戳的字幕数组
 */
export function buildSubtitleTimeline(text: string, totalDuration: number): SubtitleTimelineItem[] {
  const lines = segmentSubtitleText(text);
  if (lines.length === 0) return [];

  const totalChars = lines.reduce((sum, line) => sum + line.length, 0);
  const subtitles: SubtitleTimelineItem[] = [];
  let currentTime = 0;

  for (let i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
    const line = lines[i];
    const duration = totalChars > 0 ? (line.length / totalChars) * totalDuration : totalDuration / lines.length;
    // 最后一行确保覆盖到总时长末尾
    const endTime = i === lines.length - 1 ? totalDuration : currentTime + duration;

    // 逐字时间戳：为每个字符分配相对结束时间
    const charCount = line.length;
    const charDuration = charCount > 0 ? duration / charCount : duration;
    const charTimings: number[] = [];
    for (let c = 0; c < charCount; c++) {
      charTimings.push(currentTime + (c + 1) * charDuration);
    }

    subtitles.push({
      text: line,
      startTime: currentTime,
      endTime,
      charTimings,
    });
    currentTime = endTime;
  }

  return subtitles;
}
